Collected Speeches of Rev. Sun Myung Moon
538
Compiled by the Committee for the Compilation of Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Speeches

Foreword
In the beginning, God created the heavens and the earth with His Word, and He intended to establish Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, at the center to fulfill the ideal of the Word. However, Adam and Eve distrusted the Word and fell, resulting in a sinful world centered on Satan. Consequently, God has revealed His Word according to the development of human spirit and intellect throughout the ages, orchestrating the providence to restore the ideal of the Word. The fulfillment of God's promises through the Word has depended on human responsibility. This mainstream history has progressed through the Old Testament era led by Moses, the New Testament era led by Jesus, and has finally reached the era of the Completed Testament. The era of the Completed Testament is the age of the fulfillment of the Word, where the long-awaited ideal of God's promise is realized through the earthly manifestation of the True Parents, who are the embodiment of the completed Word.

On April 17, 1935, in his hometown of Jeongju, North Pyongan Province, during a mountaintop prayer, Rev. Sun Myung Moon had a spiritual encounter with Jesus and was officially called to the path of God's providence, marking the start of his public life. Over the next ten years, he explored both the spiritual and physical worlds, dedicating himself to prayer, truth-seeking, and experiential living, ultimately elucidating and systematizing the fundamental truth of the Principle, which is the Word of heavenly law.

Immediately after Korea's liberation in 1945, he began spreading the Word and engaging in providential activities for the restoration of the nation and the world. During this process, he endured severe persecution and misunderstanding from established religious and political circles, including six imprisonments. However, through the transformative power of living for the sake of others, which is the core value of the new Word, he naturally subdued all adversarial forces. In January 2001, he conducted the historic Coronation Ceremony for God's Kingship and achieved a significant victory by being acclaimed as the King of Peace by leaders from various fields worldwide.

Rev. Sun Myung Moon came as the embodiment of God's true love, true life, and true lineage, and through the history of the Word and Blessing, he bequeathed these to humanity. His path was that of a true parent, a true teacher, and a true owner. Throughout his life, he lived sacrificially, using the heart of a parent, the body of a servant, shedding sweat for the earth, tears for humanity, and blood for heaven. He not only illuminated profound heavenly truths and taught them day and night but also thoroughly practiced them as a model, consistently living a life of giving with the heart of true love.

Rev. Sun Myung Moon's words are an infinite source of life that awakens fallen humanity from ignorance and death. Since the counterpart of true love is created only by investing more than one's life force, he devoted his entire life and passion to giving the Word. Although the themes, levels, and scope of the Word vary according to the progressive stages of providence, the conditions of the times, and the audience, the consistent goal has been the completion of the providence of true love.

Rev. Sun Myung Moon's words have been officially recorded since April 1956 and have been supplied through documents, audio, and video media according to the practical needs and conditions of the time. In 1983, comprehensive compilation work began in earnest, and on the occasion of Rev. Sun Myung Moon's 90th birthday, a collection of 524 volumes of his speeches was published. This is an unprecedented masterpiece in history, unparalleled in both quantity and quality, and is an invaluable legacy for all humanity.

Rev. Sun Myung Moon's collection of speeches is the highest scripture, an exemplary sermon collection, and a public lecture series. Leaders from various fields in America and the world have praised Rev. Sun Myung Moon as the champion who knows best about God, Satan, humanity, the spirit world, Jesus, the Bible and scriptures, human history, and the value of the true family. Such evaluations are fully verified and proven throughout Rev. Sun Myung Moon's speeches.

The Word encompasses the essence of theories in various fields of human society, including theology, anthropology, cosmology, history, religion, politics, society, culture, and art, based on absolute values. The Word is so diverse and broad that it can be said to encompass all the major and minor themes that can be experienced in the lives of contemporary humanity. Its flow is like a majestic consistency or unity, originating from deep mountains and valleys, forming a great river, and culminating in the ocean. It is indeed like a grand journey of truth.

The composition of the Word is richly interwoven with spirituality and intellect, religious essence and scientific information, philosophical depth, and literary and poetic descriptions. It maintains a high dignity and serene comfort, passionate enthusiasm and tranquility, and like the alternation of day and night, it harmonizes sincerity and confidentiality. The captivating power of the original emotional language leads to constant admiration. There is humor and laughter that make one burst into laughter, and there are poignant stories that make one weep with sorrow. It transcends time, leading to a sense of unity that evokes empathy and emotion. It is truly the highest pinnacle of human language and the proclamation of heavenly words.

Rev. Sun Myung Moon stated that the Word is a victorious record of life, a proclamation and declaration to humanity and future history, and the mother of heavenly law. Living according to the Word allows one to enter and reside in the liberated and free realm of the Kingdom of Heaven on earth, beyond the realm of the Fall. Becoming one with the Word grants one the rights of resonance and relationship with counterparts of the same connection. Therefore, the Word possesses an absoluteness that does not permit any artificial addition or subtraction and exercises the stern power of the iron rod in history.

We, as beneficiaries of this providential grace, are truly blessed and happy to have received this invaluable treasure of eternal and unchanging value without cost. Thus, we must strive even more to create a world of peace ideal through a life of constantly reading, practicing, and spreading the Word. By doing so, we must offer infinite gratitude, praise, and glory to God and the True Parents, who are the ultimate owners of the Word, with the substantial results of our achievements.

1)
The Owner of Love
(Bowing, Family Pledge, Representative Prayer) Read this. "8th" Say it. "8th!" Now! (Reading of the speech to be given at the 1st Anniversary of the Founding of the Universal Peace Federation on September 12, titled 'Inauguration of the Universal Peace Federation Kingdom, God's Ideal Family and the Kingdom of Peace Ideal World' followed by a letter related to Hyung Jin Nim) (Applause)
We must teach the decisive conclusion of providential history to all humanity
The decisive conclusion of providential history is that there is nothing in the content that humanity can deny. It is also an unknown fact. That unknown fact is not a concept but a reality. Those who cannot acknowledge the actual fact will become dropouts in the substantial world of the spirit and physical realms. It is merciless.

Now, in the unification of the two worlds, as a reflection, each of you must undergo a great transformation with joy and gratitude; if you fall into conditions of sorrow and indemnity, it becomes a world of darkness. The sun departs. After Adam's fall, it was as if God did not exist, and even though the True Parents have clearly shown the path to the end, if one denies this, everything will be uprooted. I do not even want to imagine it. It is the same for the teacher. The word 'indemnity' should not exist. Do you understand what I mean?

This time, the three generations must take responsibility and teach all these facts to all humanity and the entire earth without leaving anyone out. Just as the 600,000 Israelites set out to restore Canaan, 6 billion, 6.5 billion people are now setting out for the original ideal land where the spirit and body are united. If they do not enter and live in the ideal land, they cannot answer to God and those who contributed to the providence centered on God. Those without answers cannot exist, not only in terms of existence value but also in symbolic, figurative, and substantial achievements. We must now make the final declaration of the universe's last stop. That will be on January 13, 2013.

At that time, you must make a great migration to the world of your original homeland drawn in your heart. The place where you were born is not your hometown. It is the land of the enemy's bloodline that made heaven lament. You must not even dream of the place divided into the spirit and physical realms, nor think of it, nor let it remain as a dream-like fact that never existed. Only then can you enter the bright noon settlement of the kingdom of heaven or the noon world, a world without shadows. Those with shadows cannot enter that world.

How much must you reflect on yourself? Of course, you must reflect and introspect, knowing well the position you are currently in. You know the difference between your mind and body not being united. There is no need for excuses. You know yourself better. You know it before God, before your parents, and before your teacher, leaving no room for denial. Without resolving to be a direct child who inherited the bloodline of God's true love, you cannot become a citizen of the kingdom of heaven. It is serious. Do you understand? "Yes."

You must clarify the theoretical basis
Yoon Tae-geun! "Yes." This speech is the conclusion, so give your evaluation. It is Peace Message VII. The entire conclusion is contained in this one. 

(Yoon Tae-geun's report; ……How to restore the enemy? By restoring the enemy with true love that loves the enemy's child more than one's own child, that is the message that resonated with me. Reflecting on the path of indemnity restoration that Father walked, naturally subjugating enemies with true love, I felt that if we practice this true love, Father's will can be fulfilled in my individual and family. This message is the core message, and I felt it deeply. I reflected on it and received much inspiration.) Explain why we must love the enemy more than our own child! Didn't I tell you the other day? "Yes." Explain it again.

(Report continues; ……Memorizing this message, I realized that Father's life was this content, and only by living this life can peace in the family, peace with neighbors, and overall peace be achieved. I felt that this message is the historical fruit, and it touched me deeply.) Explain the content. The theoretical basis!

This is not just news heard. The theoretical basis of the content, the undeniable presence of two world realms, and the need to subjugate one world to the other, you must clarify that. Otherwise, it is not understood. It passes through the clouds. You don't know if you are crossing a mountain or walking on flat ground.

When there is fog, even at sea, it feels like you are floating in the air. Even in an airplane, when you enter the clouds, you don't know if you are high or low. You thought you were going up, but you went down. You are attached to the ground. What is the theoretical basis? Like a meter that goes up, there must be something that leads in reality, but what is that theoretical basis? Explain it simply. "Yes." It is simple. It is extremely simple. (Report by Hwang Sun-jo) What is missing, Hyo-yul? (Report by Kim Hyo-yul)

Is the explanation complete? Does your heart say, "That's right!"? It is vague. It is vague. God and Satan, there are two. How should they become one? Because there are two, the mind and body fight, and because there are two, men and women fight centered on themselves. Among the two, one is the mind and the other is the body, but who started love first? God should have started first, but Satan started first.

Where is the organ of love? There is only one organ of love forever. It is God's organ. The male organ of love belongs to God, and the female organ of love should also belong to God. They don't know this now. They don't know. Satan knows, and God knows. What God knows is that the two became separate because the bloodline changed. The root, love, changed. Love is the same love. Eve's love and Adam's love went through the same course, but the bloodline changed by loving Satan, the enemy. The bloodline is important, always important, the bloodline!

Within the bloodline, there are two. One is Satan's bloodline, and the other is God's bloodline. They cannot become one. They are enemies. Then how can the enemy's bloodlines become one? By transcending the realm of the Fall and knowing only God—Satan is not even in the dream. Knowing as my own, the body and mind cannot fight as long as God exists.

When you look at it that way, are your mind and body fighting now or not? "They are fighting." That's the problem. They are fighting, but who won first? Satan won first in love, not God. It is rooted, and the influence of the body, which has a different bloodline, prevents the mind from dominating the body.

Therefore, fundamentally, this fight started with the individual and is connected to the entire history. Heaven and earth were divided because the bloodline was different, and heaven and earth can become one only if the bloodline is the same. But since Satan is in the position of the owner of the bloodline, what can be done? The owner Satan cannot be subjugated by force.

In the Garden of Eden, God, who was to establish one bloodline, says that you must not be conscious of the Fall until God's love bloodline appears worldwide. "You are in a position to receive love with me." That is the problem. Do you understand? "Yes."

The fact that your mind and body are fighting now means you do not know the Principle. Why must you love your enemy more than your own children? Satan's love is centered on a bloodline below the Fall. By loving the enemy, you return to the original position of God's love as if the Fall never happened. It is like turning a circle where the left hand becomes the right hand, and the right hand becomes the left hand.

By doing so, even if Satan defiled the bloodline, if he can say, "I loved while keeping the position of the archangel who did not defile the bloodline," then Satan's bloodline cannot exist. Do you understand? "Yes."

The concept of absolute faith, absolute love, and absolute obedience means disregarding even one's existence. Therefore, for you, the original ideal of God's creation.... If God's bloodline had entered, Satan's bloodline would never appear. Plus and plus automatically disappear. That is the natural principle.

If Satan's bloodline had not entered, the mind would never be dragged by the body. Therefore, the concept of absolute faith, absolute love, and absolute obedience is unnecessary because it is already established above that. That is how it is. You must understand this.

Then, what about you? Within you, Satan's bloodline and God's bloodline are fighting, but God's bloodline is not first. Satan's bloodline is first, so the world is connected centered on the body. It is substantial.

God is an incorporeal substance, but Satan completely occupied the substantial realm centered on the bloodline of this world. Everywhere, everything was defiled by Satan's bloodline. Then, even if Jesus' children were born, what would have happened? Jesus' children must not regard Satan as an enemy. Without a heart of love higher than the archangel's bloodline, you cannot transcend the realm of the Fall. Do you understand?

The bloodline must be overturned to be correct
Therefore, before joining the Unification Church, not only the children you were connected with but also the entire nation were connected to the bloodline realm of the body, not the bloodline through the connection of love in the mind world. When you say 'love,' it connects love and life. The father is the root of life, and the mother is the vessel. Only when these two become one does a bloodline emerge. It has never become one. When it is said to be one, Satan does not exist. The satanic world must disappear.

Therefore, those who want to die? Live! The body does not want to die. It absolutely cannot die. In my position, I cannot give up the connection from the position of parents. Next, I cannot forget that Cain killed Abel. Even though the ownership is undoubtedly God's, by occupying the bloodline, it became mine.

To find that, God denied everything, even His existence. Even if I am killed, what does not die? The original mind, which grew until the age of sixteen, did not die. Even if the original mind is completely killed, what happens? For example, even if God is put in the place of death, to overcome Satan, He must be able to love as if the Fall never happened.

Then, how does the entire world covered by the bloodline of the fallen archangel become? For fallen people, material civilization can dominate spiritual civilization. In Eden, spiritual civilization was supposed to dominate material civilization, but this was overturned, and the seed of love was planted in material things, proliferating and encompassing the entire world within the realm of material. The mind swallowed this, and now the authority of material, the authority of the body, has cut off the path to connect the bloodline of the mind world.

To do this, the bloodline of Satan, which goes down to hell, must be cut off, and the bloodline that can go up must be found. So, are you establishing the bloodline that can go up within yourself? Can you control your body one hundred percent according to your mind?

You cannot sell your father to exchange for the bloodline. You cannot exchange the bloodline by selling your grandfather, your husband, or your children. Why? Because Satan loved first, not God. Satan took everything from God by force, and God is reclaiming it. Such turmoil of the heart should not arise. Do you understand what I mean?

You must overturn this here. This is how it is, and it must be overturned. There is no objection. The bloodline that can absolutely become one must be the life, love, and bloodline of the absolute God. Do you understand? "Yes." This is the original, but for the descendants of the Fall, Satan's bloodline governs even hell. That realm is connected to hell.

Even within you, you think of the Unification Church as secondary, centered on the tradition of the Japanese people. You do not think of the Unification Church itself as primary. Why? Because you speak Japanese and are Japanese, you think of that affiliation, the visible world, as having existed first. It existed first, and believing in religion and repenting came later.

Then, when Satan is in the same position as God, the bloodline must be overturned to be correct. It is like this. Who must be overturned? Should this be overturned, or should this be overturned? When it becomes 180 degrees, it becomes 360 degrees, and it becomes like this. It completely disappears. In trying to make it completely disappear, the two positions gradually become faint and return to one position.

Think centered on yourself. Have you become like that? Are you like that or not? Can you take out your eye if told to? Can you burn your body if told to? Then, if told to burn not only your property but also the entire land of Japan, the emperor, and your parents and offer them, there is no one who can do that. As long as that lingering attachment remains... It is because I loved first.

Now, if there is a son of God, that son is the son sought after the Fall, Abel, but to find Abel, Cain must be killed. He must be eliminated. To eliminate Cain, one must have the authority to love from the individual to the universe with the love that could have united with God. Isn't that the original world?

The root must change
You must organize it within yourself. Who fell? Before the world fell, the individual fell, and I fell. What fell? Among the conscience and body, the body was loved first by Satan. Not God.

In this way, the substantial of the substantial is the body. Is the reproductive organ visible as the form of the body, or is it visible as the form of the invisible? There is a reproductive organ, right? Male and female! It is Satan's. "I used it first, not God," he says. How can you deny that? Then God Himself must be killed. It is as if God Himself was killed.

Someone like the teacher, even if God guides, will not return after hearing the Principle for an hour and a half. It is practice. "Isn't the boundary line between the body and mind not where God first became the owner of love?" That is the problem. Then the fallen humanity is the fruit of the body that loved.

You must deny this. To deny it, there are two places, and to deny one, if you love beyond that, this disappears. It was in the same position, but if God's love rises, and if it loves beyond this position and the bloodline, life, and lineage become one, then Satan's existence must disappear. Do you understand? Up to here, you understand? "Yes."

It is like this within you. According to that standard, can you control your body with your mind? You must deny everything from the individual to the family. It is up to the national level. You must go through the five stages of individual, family, tribe, people, and nation. Can you deny everything at the individual level? If it is Japan, you must burn the entire land and people of Japan, and if it does not naturally subjugate, it is an invasion by force. Fire is the strongest, so it melts before it.

What melts it? It is melted by the power of love, not by means or knowledge. With the explosive power of love, you must be willing to sell your grandfather, father, and three generations of children to return to the original standard. If the world does not become like that, I deny it and sweep it away. Satan's bloodline must disappear without a trace.

Even if you win in your heart and are in the position of noon settlement, the family is not like that. If there are twelve siblings, and they have hundreds of children, they do not obey like God, True Parents, or a teacher. Saying no means Satan is not dead. Satan must be subjugated and start retreating to be gathered and disappear where there is sunlight.

Then, with the same love as the disappeared bloodline, it cannot be. It must be higher.
Love that can illuminate the veins should begin to shine continuously from an individual's light. Even if there is only a little light in the darkness, it shines through, just like that. There is no darkness that dominates the light. When love and light appear brighter, the satanic world must automatically disappear. Therefore, when one cannot claim what they can call their own, they can connect to the value of the first love centered on Adam and Eve in the unfallen Garden of Eden, and extend to the infinite world without struggle. Only the principle of love, which can extend without struggle, can make Satan submit and follow. The world was conquered with the fruit of first love, but it cannot be eliminated with just the circumstances of the satanic world. The roots must change. Understand? "Yes."

If a higher life and love appear, the satanic world will submit. Then the issue is lineage. For lineage, love is the issue. Love is the issue, and love and life must become God's. God is the subject of love, the subject of life, and the subject of lineage. Absolute love, absolute life, absolute lineage, but a fake has appeared. These days, the mullet! The fake mullet looks exactly like the real one. Its head is even bigger. That's exactly it. Wow! Because of this, the fake mullet jumps better than the real one. Why? Because its head goes over first, and then the tail follows. When you see it, its body is plump, and the real mullet can't jump because its belly is big. It's just like that.

Therefore, at the root, if you completely settle the two masters of love in your heart and create peace, even if your family stays still, they must naturally submit. When you do what your mother couldn't do and fulfill even her wishes, she will submit. What can naturally be digested? If a higher life and higher love cannot appear, the satanic world cannot submit. It cannot disappear, but only higher love can make it submit, so if you enter the original standard of love and enter God's eternal kingdom, what happens? When you enter the kingdom and are given the qualification of an archangel, there is no change in your heart. You must establish it this way, saying, "Originally, I must serve the master, so I repent for stealing everything from you and return it all." You must stamp it and return it. It's not coercion. It's a heart of love.

Therefore, what happens when the True Parents appear? Because true love, true life, and true lineage have been the absolute masters from the beginning, when those words appear to you, if you hold onto them for 1 year, 2 years... 21 years, you can naturally digest your body and the nation and world. It's a natural law. If you become someone who can do that, it's cross-marriage, replacement marriage. Cross-marriage is not the issue. Replacement marriage sweeps everything away at once. You know the formula principle, so...! Then you love your enemy more than your own children.

How many enemies are there! In the five stages of the individual, family, tribe, people, and nation, the enemy realm is finally subdued by this formula. It must be subdued just like the principle that subdued the body and mind. Then it's the same between husband and wife. The couple is also enemies. When the standard of the mind is ahead, you educate and digest it centered on the standard of the mind, naturally submitting before your husband, and then both of you do the same with your children.

Children are also enemies. When children are enemies, if you stand in the position of sacrificing even your life and continue eternally, the position of parents and children can become one centered on eternity. Therefore, there is no way other than natural submission.

A fake cannot coexist with the real. Therefore, does the archangel's lineage have the qualification to participate in the ideal Adam's lineage world? "Yes." No! "Yes!" So your thoughts are wrong. How can the love of the archangel and God's love, Adam's love, be the same? The lineage is different. You must know that the lineage has changed. It's always an exchange. It must revolve like this, but it can't revolve like this. If it revolves, everything around it disappears. It is destroyed.

When you look at it centered on such principles, even the children born from blessed families are not real children. After changing the lineage, holding the sanctification ceremony, what next? You must return to the Adam family at the top of the world and solve the issues of lineage, Cain and Abel, and ownership. When you enter there and say, "That's nothing. I don't need thousands of times more. From beginning to end, God, you are the master," then automatically, the earthly kingdom and the heavenly kingdom become one.

That's what you must do. You must clearly know what the two masters are. It's not about what the external world is like, sacrificing this or that. It's about correcting this foundation and standing in the position of God's master, completely suppressing the satanic world's lineage, even to hell. Until you create the standard of love that God loved, Satan will not submit.

Therefore, unless you love more than your own children, your own country, or anything else, there is no way to make it submit. If you correct just this, it will fit no matter what. Understand? "Yes." It's not like that, right? It's a fact that it's not like that.

At that time, because the false master carried the bundle of love, life, and ownership, what happens? If you come out with a pure bundle of love, life, and lineage without a speck of dust, Satan will submit. Satan has a fake bundle of lineage, life, and love. You must know that a fake cannot coexist with the real. The lineage, the root, is different. Understand? "Yes."

So, even your children cannot go to the kingdom. When you complete all these procedures and the parents shout "Mansei," the world will rumble... Heaven and earth will also shout "Mansei!" That's why they say "Eokmanse." There is only one place where you can shout "Eokmanse." It's not a place where you can shout "Eokmanse" anywhere. Even if an individual shouts "Eokcheonmanse, Eok-eokmanse" from a position above the cosmos, it's okay. Otherwise, it gets blocked. Understand? "Yes."

Now, if from the mother's position, she says, "Oh! I hate the teacher's love, the teacher's life, the teacher's lineage!" it disappears. The lineage has changed. What was like this must be matched like this. Because it's a woman, it doesn't work like this, so you do it like this. At the same position of plus and minus, there is repulsion. It must be matched so that it can conform like this, and the man should not match it. God must come down and match it.

Isn't it the same for you? You think it would be nice to do as you please, right? "God or whatever, mother and father or whatever, the law of the country or whatever, as I please..." But where is "as I please"? There are two masters of the lineage, so one must disappear. Do you understand this? Through the Unification Principle, you clearly know the false lineage, false life, and false bloodline.

Peace is achieved through True Parents. Many of you women, why did you come to find Reverend Moon of the Unification Church? Is it because he is handsome, rich, or skilled? Why is that? Original love! God has all kinds of personalities, but what is the attribute? When you say "mainstream," it means the original bloodline. The bloodline realm is the absolute of absolutes. It must remain forever.

Isn't that so? Would it be nice if your mother and father disappeared forever? Children say it would be nice to reach the highest position. Why didn't that happen? The satanic lineage was not sorted out. To sort out the lineage, what the teacher is doing at this last moment is lineage conversion. The organ of love should stop playing games that Satan likes and find a lineage that keeps purity. Did you find it? Did you find it or not? "We found it." So, were children born in pure love? "Yes." At that time, did the body and mind not fight? "They fought." If they fought, it's not purity. (Laughter) That's how it is.

Even though the teacher is now in the high position of the Savior, Messiah, Second Coming, and True Parents, he doesn't go to that position. Until he escapes this, he stays still and watches. If I were in the same position as them, I could kill them if they didn't listen. No, I just leave them and change their clothes again. I bathe them and change them into clean clothes. Even if I change them a thousand or ten thousand times, they must say, "No matter how good the clothes are, there is nothing to choose from, and it's good just to be by your side." That's how it should be.

So, the women of the Unification Church all disliked the marriage given by the teacher. Even if they go to the cemetery, they want to be buried where the teacher is buried, so why move the grave separately? They want to enter an absolute grave, in one place, and dislike anything else.

Therefore, the Unification Church members in Japan made a joint cemetery by burying them in the earth, right? Do they do it like in Japan, or like in a shrine? They prepare it every day in the kamidana (household shrine) and live with it as if with their parents. How unfilial and disloyal is that! In the family, it's unfilial, in the country, it's disloyal, and in the world, it's treason. It's worse than Satan.

Did Adam and Eve know they could become traitors in the Garden of Eden? They thought loving Eve was simple, but it was such a big issue. After committing it, they didn't know it would be like that. When they enter prison and stay with death row inmates, they think, "Oh, if only I hadn't said that at that time. If only I hadn't listened to that, I wouldn't be here..." They can't escape it. "Why did I listen to that, why didn't I realize it?" they think.

The teacher told you everything through the words, but do you know it now for the first time? You fight, right? What do you say? "We fight." Or do you say, "We don't fight"? A Japanese person cannot become an American. Even after thousands of years, they cannot. But a Japanese person can become a heavenly person. Why? Because the returning Lord becomes the True Parents...! The first master planted a fake lineage, but the returning Lord clears it up, cleans it thoroughly, and saves the world.

Religions fight too, right? Those who fight have nothing to do with the True Parents. Confucianism, Islam, Buddhism, and Christianity fight, right? Religions fight each other. Then the chosen people and the non-chosen people fight, right? God cannot come to a place where there is fighting. Who brings peace to that? The True Parents must come.

Even though they don't know religion and oppose it, even though they oppose the Unification Church, when they know the words of the True Parents, their hearts are moved, and they want to go quickly to the True Parents. They want to follow quickly. Even if there are many people in front, they don't sleep or eat and urge to go quickly. Isn't it the same for you?

If you follow the teacher, you will be liberated. Yesterday, the teacher came from Geomundo and went out to the sea again.
